	is_triggered_only = yes

			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_national_committee.02.a executed"
		name = china_national_committee.02.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

}

#### SAR Events
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.001
	title = china_sar.001.t
	desc = china_sar.001.d
	picture = GFX_politics_talks
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_sar.001.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.001.a executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CHI
			modifier = CSSTA
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TAI
			modifier = CSSTA
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CHI
			modifier = large_commercial_relations
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TAI
			modifier = large_commercial_relations
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_TAI_shared_modifier } } }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_TAI_shared_modifier }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_TAI_shared_modifier }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_democratic_drift = -0.02 tooltip = democratic_drift_tt }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_civilian_factories_productivity = 0.03 tooltip = civilian_factories_productivity_tt }
		set_country_flag = TAI_CSSTA_signed
		CHI = { add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 10 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.001.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.001.b executed"
		CHI = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = -5 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust < 0 } }
				set_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 0 }
			}
		}
	}

}

#Cross-Strait Business Networks
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.002
	title = china_sar.002.t
	desc = china_sar.002.d
	picture = GFX_politics_talks
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_sar.002.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.002.a executed"
		add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^1 = 0.02 }
		add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^2 = -0.01 }
		recalculate_party = yes
		CHI = { add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 8 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.002.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.002.b executed"
		CHI = { add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 3 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.002.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.002.c executed"
		add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^2 = 0.01 }
		recalculate_party = yes
		add_war_support = 0.03
		CHI = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = -8 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust < 0 } }
				set_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 0 }
			}
		}
	}

}

#Beijing's Interference Operations Exposed
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.005
	title = china_sar.005.t
	desc = china_sar.005.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_sign_treaty1
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_sar.005.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.005.a executed"
		set_country_flag = { flag = TAI_foreign_interference days = 180 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = political_outreach
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = political_outreach
		}
		CHI = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = -15 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust < 0 } }
				set_variable = { CHI_TAI_trust = 0 }
			}
			country_event = { id = china_sar.006 days = 3 }
		}
	}

}

# Level 1 Incident — Dangerous Approach
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.007
	title = china_sar.007.t
	desc = china_sar.007.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Deny involvement — tension cools but future incidents escalate
	option = {
		name = china_sar.007.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.007.a executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_strait_tension = -3 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension min = 0 max = 100 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = CHI_recent_provocation days = 30 value = 1 }
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.007.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.007.b executed"
		set_country_flag = { flag = CHI_recent_provocation days = 30 value = 1 }
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.007.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.007.c executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_strait_tension = 3 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension min = 0 max = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = -2 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = CHI_recent_provocation days = 30 value = 1 }
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
	}

	# Stay silent — no change
	# Publicly defend the action — tension rises, support drops

}

# Level 2 Incident — Naval Collision
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.008
	title = china_sar.008.t
	desc = china_sar.008.d
	picture = x
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Blame America — 50/50 escalation or deflection
	option = {
		name = china_sar.008.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.008.a executed"
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				# US responds hard — support surges
				add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = 8 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
				clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
				add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_strait_tension = 5 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension_tt }
				clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension min = 0 max = 100 }
			}
			50 = {
				# Blows over — minor tension reduction
				add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = -3 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
				clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = CHI_recent_provocation days = 60 value = 1 }
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.008.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.008.b executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_strait_tension = 5 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension min = 0 max = 100 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = CHI_recent_provocation days = 60 value = 1 }
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.008.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.008.c executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_strait_tension = -6 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension min = 0 max = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = 3 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = CHI_recent_provocation days = 60 value = 1 }
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
	}

	# Stay silent — tension rises
	# Private apologies — de-escalation, but support rebounds

}

# Congress Arms Vote — Lobby opportunity
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.012
	title = china_sar.012.t
	desc = china_sar.012.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Activate lobby network — 70% block arms sale
	option = {
		name = china_sar.012.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.012.a executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = -5 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
				clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
			}
			30 = {
				# Lobby fails — support rebounds
				add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = 3 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
				clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.012.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.012.b executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = -3 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_strait_tension = 2 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension min = 0 max = 100 }
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.012.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.012.c executed"
		TAI = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TAI_civil_defense_readiness
				days = 365
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}

	# Economic threats — minor support drop, tension rises
	# Do nothing — Taiwan gets arms deal buff

}

# Taiwan Considers Capitulation (full blockade, low US support) — fires to TAI
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.017
	title = china_sar.017.t
	desc = china_sar.017.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Refuse to surrender — fight on
	option = {
		name = china_sar.017.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.017.a executed"
		add_war_support = 0.15
		add_stability = -0.10
		CHI = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_strait_tension = 10 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_strait_tension min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				CHI = { check_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support < 15 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.017.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.017.b executed"
		trigger = {
			CHI = { check_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support < 20 } }
		}
		CHI = {
			country_event = { id = china_sar.018 days = 7 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				CHI = { check_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support < 15 } }
			}
		}
	}

	# Begin negotiations with Beijing

}

# Taiwan Enters Negotiations — fires to CHI after TAI accepts talks
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.018
	title = china_sar.018.t
	desc = china_sar.018.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_sign_treaty1
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept peaceful reunification
	option = {
		name = china_sar.018.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.018.a executed"
		annex_country = { target = TAI transfer_troops = yes }
		add_stability = 0.10
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_political_power = 200
		clr_country_flag = CHI_TAI_full_blockade_active
		clr_country_flag = CHI_TAI_partial_blockade_active
		clr_country_flag = CHI_TAI_maritime_zone_active
	}

}

# Crisis Mode — Tension Hits 100
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.019
	title = china_sar.019.t
	desc = china_sar.019.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_military
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# De-escalate — pull back from the brink
	option = {
		name = china_sar.019.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.019.a executed"
		set_variable = { CHI_taiwan_strait_tension = 60 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = 5 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				check_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support < 30 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_sar.019.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_sar.019.b executed"
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = TAI
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_TAI_intl_isolation
		add_to_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support = 10 tooltip = CHI_taiwan_us_support_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_taiwan_us_support min = 0 max = 100 }
		add_stability = -0.10
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				check_variable = { CHI_taiwan_us_support < 30 }
			}
		}
	}

	# Push through — wargoal with heavy international penalties

}

# Taiwan Receives Ultimatum — fires to TAI
country_event = {
	id = china_sar.020
	title = china_sar.020.t
	desc = china_sar.020.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_military
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Refuse — notify China
	option = {

# China is demanding that we choose a side — CSTO split
country_event = {
	id = CHI_sco.10
	title = CHI_sco.10.t
	desc = CHI_sco.10.d
	picture = GFX_CHI_generic
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Join the SCO
	option = {
		name = CHI_sco.10.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_sco.10.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		CHI_sco_promote_to_member = yes
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = diplomatic_support
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value > 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value > 100 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_sco.10.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_sco.10.b executed"
		CHI_sco_remove = yes
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = has_expressed_loyalty
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = resisted_territorial_ambition
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_sco.10.c
		trigger = {
			has_opinion = { target = CHI value > 0 }
			has_opinion = { target = SOV value > 0 }
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_sco.10.c executed"
		CHI_sco_remove = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = non_aligned_post_csto
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
	}

	# Stay loyal to Moscow
	# Remain neutral

}

		if = { limit = { country_exists = USA } USA = { if = { limit = { has_idea = CHI_regional_crisis_alert } remove_ideas = CHI_regional_crisis_alert } } }
		if = { limit = { country_exists = JAP } JAP = { if = { limit = { has_idea = CHI_regional_crisis_alert } remove_ideas = CHI_regional_crisis_alert } } }
		if = { limit = { country_exists = KOR } KOR = { if = { limit = { has_idea = CHI_regional_crisis_alert } remove_ideas = CHI_regional_crisis_alert } } }
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_major = yes }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_peace_in_korea_delivered }
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
	}

}

# CHI_foreign.66 — Operation New Dawn Exposed (raid failure — worst outcome)
# Fires to both actor (CHI) and victim (NKO) — behavior branches on original_tag
country_event = {
	id = CHI_foreign.66
	title = CHI_foreign.66.t
	desc = CHI_foreign.66.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_military_equipment
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Event CHI_foreign.66"
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_foreign.66.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_foreign.66.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = CHI }
			set_country_flag = NKO_exposed_chinese_coup
			# Deep networks soften the fallout — assets go dark instead of being rolled up.
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_nko_internal_influence > 60 } }
				add_political_power = -100
				add_stability = -0.02
				add_to_variable = { CHI_korea_peninsula_tension = 30 tooltip = CHI_korea_peninsula_tension_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = -200
				add_stability = -0.05
				add_to_variable = { CHI_korea_peninsula_tension = 50 tooltip = CHI_korea_peninsula_tension_tt }
			}
		}
		else = {
			# NKO scope
			create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = CHI }
			declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = annex_everything }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_attempted_coup }
		}
	}

}

	}

		name = CHI_foreign.67.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_foreign.67.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = CHI }
			# With a strong internal network, enough operatives exfiltrate to preserve the position.
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_nko_internal_influence > 60 } }
				add_political_power = -50
				add_command_power = -10
				add_to_variable = { CHI_korea_peninsula_tension = 10 tooltip = CHI_korea_peninsula_tension_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = -100
				add_command_power = -20
				add_to_variable = { CHI_korea_peninsula_tension = 20 tooltip = CHI_korea_peninsula_tension_tt }
			}
		}
		else = {
			# NKO scope
			if = {
				limit = { CHI = { check_variable = { CHI_nko_internal_influence > 60 } } }
				add_stability = -0.10
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -0.05
			}
		}
	}

}

# CHI_foreign.68 — Pyongyang in Flames: Civil War (success)

	desc = CHI_foreign.68.d

	}

		name = CHI_foreign.68.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_foreign.68.a executed"

			limit = { original_tag = CHI }
			add_political_power = -50
			add_to_variable = { CHI_korea_peninsula_tension = 30 tooltip = CHI_korea_peninsula_tension_tt }
			set_country_flag = CHI_nko_civil_war_sponsor
		}
		else = {
			# NKO scope — civil war size scales with CHI's internal influence
			if = {
				limit = { CHI = { check_variable = { CHI_nko_internal_influence > 80 } } }
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = communism
					size = 0.7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { CHI = { check_variable = { CHI_nko_internal_influence > 60 } } }
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = communism
					size = 0.55
				}
			}
			else = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = communism
					size = 0.4
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

# CHI_foreign.69 — A New Dawn in Pyongyang (critical success — clean coup → puppet)
# Fires to both actor (CHI) and victim (NKO)
country_event = {
	id = CHI_foreign.69
	title = CHI_foreign.69.t
	desc = CHI_foreign.69.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politics
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Event CHI_foreign.69"
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_foreign.69.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_foreign.69.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = CHI }
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_to_variable = { CHI_korea_peninsula_tension = -20 tooltip = CHI_korea_peninsula_tension_tt }
			set_country_flag = CHI_coup_succeeded
			# At overwhelming internal influence, CHI reabsorbs NKO directly rather than puppeting.
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_nko_internal_influence > 80 } }
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_owned_by = NKO }
					CHI = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = NKO
					autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet_state
					end_wars = no
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			# NKO scope — skip regime idea if we're being annexed outright.
			if = {
				limit = { CHI = { NOT = { check_variable = { CHI_nko_internal_influence > 80 } } } }
				add_ideas = NKO_pro_beijing_regime
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = USA }
				USA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = NKO modifier = CHI_nko_regime_change_opinion } }
				NKO = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = CHI_nko_regime_change_opinion } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = KOR }
				KOR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = NKO modifier = CHI_nko_regime_change_opinion } }
				NKO = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = CHI_nko_regime_change_opinion } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = JAP }
				JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = NKO modifier = CHI_nko_regime_change_opinion } }
				NKO = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = CHI_nko_regime_change_opinion } }
			}
		}
	}

}

	desc = china_scs.10.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_naval
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.10.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.10.a executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = territorial_integrity_violation }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = PHI
					original_tag = VIE
					original_tag = MAY
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -10
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

}

# china_scs.12 — Standoff Concluded (country event to CHI, fired by standoff decisions on completion)
country_event = {
	id = china_scs.12
	title = china_scs.12.t
	desc = china_scs.12.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_naval
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.12.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.12.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scarborough_won }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 2 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = -2 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
			add_stability = 0.02
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scarborough_contested }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = -1 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
			add_ideas = CHI_scs_setback
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = -2 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = -3 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
			add_ideas = CHI_scs_setback
			add_stability = -0.02
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

}

# china_scs.13 — Washington Responds to Chinese Encroachment (country event to USA)
# Fired when CHI_chinese_aggression > 20 or when a standoff completes

	title = china_scs.13.t
	desc = china_scs.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_military
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.13.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.13.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = { country_event = { id = china_scs.14 days = 30 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_idea = super_power
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				check_variable = { interest_rate > 6 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_scs.13.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.13.b executed"
		add_political_power = 10
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				has_idea = super_power
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { interest_rate > 6 }
			}
		}
	}

}

# china_scs.14 — PLAN Response to FONOP (country event to CHI, recurring)
country_event = {
	id = china_scs.14
	title = china_scs.14.t
	desc = china_scs.14.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_naval
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.14.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.14.a executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = -2 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = 1 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = CHI_chinese_aggression
						value = 15
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = china_scs.14 days = 180 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_government = democratic
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				check_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression > 30 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_scs.14.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.14.b executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = CHI_chinese_aggression
						value = 15
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = china_scs.14 days = 180 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_idea = super_power
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_scs.14.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.14.c executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 3 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = -3 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				85 = {}
				15 = { country_event = { id = china_scs.15 days = 7 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = CHI_chinese_aggression
						value = 15
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = china_scs.14 days = 180 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				check_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression > 30 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -15
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
	}

}

# china_scs.15 — South Sea Incident (country event, fires to both CHI and USA)
# When CHI receives it: applies variable and idea effects. When USA receives it: diplomatic response only.
country_event = {
	id = china_scs.15
	title = china_scs.15.t
	desc = china_scs.15.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_naval
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.15.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.15.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = CHI }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = -1 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
			add_ideas = CHI_regional_crisis_alert
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = USA }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = territorial_integrity_violation }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = CHI }
				USA = { country_event = { id = china_scs.15 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_scs.15.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.15.b executed"
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = CHI }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = -2 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
			add_ideas = CHI_regional_crisis_alert
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = USA }
			add_political_power = -20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = CHI }
				USA = { country_event = { id = china_scs.15 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
	}

}

		name = china_scs.20.a

			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }

				has_government = democratic
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.20.a executed"
		name = china_scs.20.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = CHI }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
			NOT = { has_government = democratic }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
		}
	}

	option = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.20.a executed"
		name = china_scs.20.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = CHI }
			is_in_faction_with = CHI
		}
	}

}

# china_scs.52 — Ultimatum Delivered (country event to claimant, fired by decisions)
country_event = {
	id = china_scs.52
	title = china_scs.52.t
	desc = china_scs.52.d
	picture = GFX_politics_negotiations
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.52.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.52.a executed"
		add_ideas = CHI_national_humiliation
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = 3 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = VIE }
			CHI = { transfer_state = 813 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = PHI }
			CHI = { transfer_state = 943 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = MAY }
			CHI = { transfer_state = 526 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value > 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value < 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				num_of_naval_factories < 4
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_scs.52.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.52.b executed"
		add_ideas = CHI_defiance_of_china
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = territorial_integrity_violation }
			if = {
				limit = { PREV = { original_tag = VIE } }
				set_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_VIE
			}
			if = {
				limit = { PREV = { original_tag = PHI } }
				set_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_PHI
			}
			if = {
				limit = { PREV = { original_tag = MAY } }
				set_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_MAY
			}
			set_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_any
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = VIE }
				CHI = {
					start_border_war = {
						change_state_after_war = no
						attacker = {
							state = 531
							num_provinces = 1
							on_win = china_scs.56
							on_lose = china_scs.58
						}
						defender = {
							state = 813
							num_provinces = 1
							on_win = china_scs.57
							on_lose = china_scs.56
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = PHI }
				CHI = {
					start_border_war = {
						change_state_after_war = no
						attacker = {
							state = 531
							num_provinces = 1
							on_win = china_scs.56
							on_lose = china_scs.58
						}
						defender = {
							state = 943
							num_provinces = 1
							on_win = china_scs.57
							on_lose = china_scs.56
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = MAY }
				CHI = {
					start_border_war = {
						change_state_after_war = no
						attacker = {
							state = 531
							num_provinces = 1
							on_win = china_scs.56
							on_lose = china_scs.58
						}
						defender = {
							state = 526
							num_provinces = 1
							on_win = china_scs.57
							on_lose = china_scs.56
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value < 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value > 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				num_of_naval_factories < 4
			}
		}
	}

}

# china_scs.53 — Washington Weighs In (country event to USA, fired by .56 or .57.b after the claimant refuses CHI ultimatum)
# FROM = CHI scope at fire time. Claimant identity read from CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_* flags on CHI.
country_event = {
	id = china_scs.53
	title = china_scs.53.t
	desc = china_scs.53.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_military
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Option A — Issue Joint Ultimatum
	option = {
		name = china_scs.53.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.53.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = { country_event = { id = china_scs.54 days = 7 } }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_ACCEPT
		effect_tooltip = {
			CHI = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_VIE }
					transfer_state = 813
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_PHI }
					transfer_state = 943
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_MAY }
					transfer_state = 526
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_REJECT
		effect_tooltip = {
			USA = { create_wargoal = { type = liberate_wargoal target = CHI } }
			JAP = { add_war_support = 0.05 }
			RAJ = { add_war_support = 0.05 }
			AST = { add_war_support = 0.05 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = VIE
					is_in_faction_with = PHI
					is_in_faction_with = MAY
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				naval_strength_comparison = {
					other = CHI
					ratio > 1.2
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					VIE = { has_opinion = { target = USA value > 25 } }
					PHI = { has_opinion = { target = USA value > 25 } }
					MAY = { has_opinion = { target = USA value > 25 } }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				CHI = { num_of_naval_factories > 18 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_country_flag = CHI_scs_china_already_lost_border_war
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_scs.53.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.53.b executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = territorial_integrity_violation }
		CHI = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 3 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = -5 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				OR = {
					VIE = { has_opinion = { target = USA value < 0 } }
					PHI = { has_opinion = { target = USA value < 0 } }
					MAY = { has_opinion = { target = USA value < 0 } }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -15
				has_country_flag = CHI_scs_china_already_lost_border_war
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_scs.53.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.53.c executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = military_cooperation }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = VIE
					is_in_faction_with = PHI
					is_in_faction_with = MAY
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				NOT = {
					naval_strength_comparison = {
						other = CHI
						ratio > 1.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				has_country_flag = CHI_scs_china_already_lost_border_war
			}
		}
	}

	# Option B — Diplomatic Protest Only
	# Option C — Stay Out of This

}

# china_scs.56 — The Spratly Skirmish (news event, fires to CHI when CHI wins border war)
# on_win hook from start_border_war in .52.b. ROOT = CHI, FROM = the defeated claimant.
news_event = {
	id = china_scs.56
	title = china_scs.56.t
	desc = china_scs.56.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_naval
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.56.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.56.a executed"
		trigger = { original_tag = CHI }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 3 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = 2 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_VIE }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 813 } }
				transfer_state = 813
			}
			add_state_core = 813
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_PHI }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 943 } }
				transfer_state = 943
			}
			add_state_core = 943
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_MAY }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 526 } }
				transfer_state = 526
			}
			add_state_core = 526
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = { country_event = { id = china_scs.53 days = 7 } }
		}
	}

	option = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.56.a executed"
		name = china_scs.56.a
		trigger = { NOT = { original_tag = CHI } }
	}

}

# china_scs.54 — Beijing's Response to the Joint Ultimatum (country event to CHI, fired by .53.a)
country_event = {
	id = china_scs.54
	title = china_scs.54.t
	desc = china_scs.54.d
	picture = GFX_politics_negotiations
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.54.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.54.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_VIE }
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 813 }
				transfer_state = 813
				VIE = { add_state_core = 813 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_VIE
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_PHI }
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 943 }
				transfer_state = 943
				PHI = { add_state_core = 943 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_PHI
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_MAY }
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 526 }
				transfer_state = 526
				MAY = { add_state_core = 526 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_MAY
		}
		clr_country_flag = CHI_scs_ultimatum_issued_any
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = -8 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = 5 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
		add_timed_idea = { idea = CHI_national_humiliation days = 365 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				num_of_naval_factories < 12
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				check_variable = {
					var = CHI_chinese_aggression
					value = 35
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = china_scs.54.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.54.b executed"
		create_wargoal = { type = liberate_wargoal target = USA }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 10 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_scs_framework = -15 tooltip = CHI_scs_framework_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_scs_framework min = -50 max = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = { add_war_support = 0.05 }
			JAP = { add_war_support = 0.05 }
			RAJ = { add_war_support = 0.05 }
			AST = { add_war_support = 0.05 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10

# china_scs.60 — The Quad Convenes (news event, fires when CHI_chinese_aggression > 30 and quad not yet formed)
news_event = {
	id = china_scs.60
	title = china_scs.60.t
	desc = china_scs.60.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_military
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	option = {
		name = china_scs.60.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.60.a executed"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = USA
				original_tag = JAP
				original_tag = RAJ
				original_tag = AST
			}
		}
		USA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = RAJ modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = AST modifier = military_cooperation }
		}
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = RAJ modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = AST modifier = military_cooperation }
		}
		RAJ = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = AST modifier = military_cooperation }
		}
		AST = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = military_cooperation }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = RAJ modifier = military_cooperation }
		}
		add_war_support = 0.03
		CHI = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 2 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
			clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		}
	}

	option = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: china_scs.60.a executed"
		name = china_scs.60.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = USA }
			NOT = { original_tag = JAP }
			NOT = { original_tag = RAJ }
			NOT = { original_tag = AST }
		}
	}

}

# sino_indian.1 — Doklam Standoff reaction
# Fired by CHI_Doklam_Road_Standoff to BHU (and RAJ when RAJ guarantees BHU).
# Option layout: BHU gets a/b/e; RAJ gets c (defers to BHU) and d (own action).
country_event = {
	id = sino_indian.1
	title = sino_indian.1.t
	desc = sino_indian.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_military
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# BHU option A — send troops (resist)
	option = {
		name = sino_indian.1.a
		trigger = { original_tag = BHU }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sino_indian.1.a executed"
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = CHI
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value < -25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				is_in_faction_with = RAJ
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sino_indian.1.b
		trigger = { original_tag = BHU }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sino_indian.1.b executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_doklam_concession }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = RAJ }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sino_indian.1.e
		trigger = { original_tag = BHU }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sino_indian.1.e executed"
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = CHI
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = RAJ modifier = territorial_integrity_violation }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sino_indian.1.c
		trigger = { original_tag = RAJ }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sino_indian.1.c executed"
		add_war_support = 0.05
		give_guarantee = BHU
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_opinion = { target = CHI value < -10 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sino_indian.1.d
		trigger = { original_tag = RAJ }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sino_indian.1.d executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = BHU modifier = territorial_integrity_violation }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = { target = BHU value > 30 }
			}
		}
	}

	# BHU option B — do nothing
	# BHU option E — defend without allies
	# RAJ option C — protectors rally
	# RAJ option D — cannot intervene

}

# sino_indian.20 — Operation Mountain Tiger framing
# Fired by CHI_Joint_Operations to CHI.
country_event = {
	id = sino_indian.20
	title = sino_indian.20.t
	desc = sino_indian.20.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_military
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sino_indian.20.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sino_indian.20.a executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 1 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		create_faction_from_template = faction_template_sco
		PAK = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
				CHI = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_econ }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_pol }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_mil }
				}
				CHI_sco_promote_to_member = yes
			}
		}
		AFG = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
				CHI = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_econ }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_pol }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_mil }
				}
				CHI_sco_promote_to_member = yes
			}
		}
		TAJ = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
				CHI = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_econ }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_pol }
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_sco_member_mil }
				}
				CHI_sco_promote_to_member = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = PAK
						original_tag = TAJ
						original_tag = AFG
					}
				}
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = {
					var = CHI_chinese_aggression
					value = 0
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sino_indian.20.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sino_indian.20.b executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 3 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			PAK = { country_event = { id = sino_indian.46 days = 2 } }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
					NOT = { original_tag = CHI }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = aggressive_diplomacy_penalty }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = {
					var = CHI_chinese_aggression
					value = 5
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sino_indian.20.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sino_indian.20.c executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 5 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = CHI
					original_tag = PAK
					original_tag = TAJ
					original_tag = AFG
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = CHI_war_footing_central_asia
				days = 730
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {

			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
					NOT = { original_tag = CHI }
				}

					value = 10

			add_breakthrough_points = { specialization = specialization_air value = 1 }
			clr_country_flag = CHI_joint_mil_air
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_joint_mil_naval }
			add_breakthrough_points = { specialization = specialization_naval value = 1 }
			clr_country_flag = CHI_joint_mil_naval
		}

			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_joint_mil_nuclear }
			add_breakthrough_points = { specialization = specialization_nuclear value = 1 }
			clr_country_flag = CHI_joint_mil_nuclear
		}
	}

# CHI_foreign.200 — The Fleets Are at the Line (CHI receiver)
# Fired by CHI_the_senkaku_crisis focus completion.
country_event = {
	id = CHI_foreign.200
	title = CHI_foreign.200.t
	desc = CHI_foreign.200.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_naval
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = CHI
	}

	# Option A — Force the issue: fires the JAP receiver and USA receiver, escalates aggression.
	option = {
		name = CHI_foreign.200.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_foreign.200.a executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_chinese_aggression = 5 tooltip = CHI_chinese_aggression_tt }
		clamp_variable = { var = CHI_chinese_aggression min = -50 max = 50 }
		JAP = { country_event = { id = CHI_foreign.201 days = 1 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_ACCEPT
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = { transfer_state = 939 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_REJECT
		effect_tooltip = {
			create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state_focus
				target = JAP
				generator = { 939 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { has_guaranteed = JAP } }
			USA = { country_event = { id = CHI_foreign.215 days = 2 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = {
					var = CHI_chinese_aggression
					value = 10
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_foreign.200.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_foreign.200.b executed"
		set_country_flag = CHI_senkaku_probe_only
		add_stability = 0.05
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = border_tensions }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = {
					var = CHI_chinese_aggression
					value = 0
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				check_variable = {
					var = CHI_chinese_aggression
					value = 10
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_foreign.200.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CHI_foreign.200.c executed"
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { original_tag = JAP }
				NOT = { original_tag = CHI }
			}
			news_event = { id = CHI_foreign.203 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { has_guaranteed = JAP } }
			USA = { country_event = { id = CHI_foreign.202 days = 2 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = {
					var = CHI_chinese_aggression
					value = 0
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Option B — Probe and withdraw: restrained signal, stability gain, opinion penalty on JAP.
	# Option C — Demand UN mediation: news to neutrals, USA decides whether to honour guarantee.

}

				factor = 0

			}
		}
	}

			}

				add = 10

			}

				add = -20

			}
		}
	}

	option = {

		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30

				add = 30
				any_country = { has_guaranteed = JAP }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = nationalist
			}
		}
	}

	# Option B — Mobilise: CHI receives a wargoal on 939 and war may follow.
	# Option C — Request US intervention: fires CHI_foreign.202 with a flag marking JAP as requesting help.

}

# chi_bri.1 -- The Astana Speech (onboarding, fired by CHI_Belt_and_Road_Initiative focus)
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.1
	title = chi_bri.1.t
	desc = chi_bri.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.1.a executed"
		add_political_power = 50
		set_country_flag = CHI_bri_active
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_treasury = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_monthly_income = 5 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_monthly_returns = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_returns_bri_pct = 1.0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_returns_multiplier = 1 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_active_projects = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_completed_projects = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_defaulted_projects = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_project_slots = 3 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_pending_applications = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_global_presence = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_predatory_score = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_winwin_score = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_africa_engagement = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_southasia_engagement = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_centralasia_engagement = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_seasia_engagement = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_europe_engagement = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_latam_engagement = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_meast_engagement = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_ports_built = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_railways_built = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_pipelines_built = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_telecom_built = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_mines_secured = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_powerplants_built = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_industrial_zones = 0 }
		set_variable = { CHI_bri_prestige_projects = 0 }

		set_variable = { CHI_bri_telecom_tier_discount = 0 }

		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

# chi_bri.10 -- Application Review (CHI receives from applicant via recipient decision)
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.10
	title = chi_bri.10.t
	desc = chi_bri.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = CHI
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.10.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.10.a executed"
		FROM = {
			set_temp_variable = { application_terms = 1 }
			BRI_handle_application = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_ACCEPT
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bri_partner_tier_1 }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_bri_returns_multiplier_temp = 0.05 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				FROM = { has_government = communism }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				FROM = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.10.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.10.b executed"
		FROM = {
			set_temp_variable = { application_terms = 2 }
			BRI_handle_application = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_ACCEPT
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bri_partner_tier_1 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				FROM = {
					has_opinion = { target = CHI value < 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.10.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.10.c executed"
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = CHI_Predatory_Lending_Doctrine
		}
		FROM = {
			set_temp_variable = { application_terms = 3 }
			BRI_handle_application = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_ACCEPT
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bri_partner_tier_1 }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_predatory_score = 1 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 6
				has_completed_focus = CHI_Predatory_Lending_Doctrine
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.10.d
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.10.d executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { CHI_bri_active_projects > 13 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { has_government = communism }
			}
		}
	}
}

# chi_bri.11 -- Project Completion (CHI scope, FROM = recipient)
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.11
	title = chi_bri.11.t
	desc = chi_bri.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politics
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = CHI
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			60 = { set_variable = { chi_bri_outcome = 1 } }
			25 = { set_variable = { chi_bri_outcome = 2 } }
			15 = { set_variable = { chi_bri_outcome = 3 } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.11.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.11.a executed"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = chi_bri_outcome
				value = 1
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_temp_variable = { project_type = ROOT.chi_bri_project_type }
			BRI_select_target_state = yes
			BRI_register_and_recalc_partner = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_active_projects = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_completed_projects = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_global_presence = 5 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 8 } }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_monthly_returns = 3 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 1 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 2 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 3 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 5 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 6 }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_monthly_returns = 2 }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_monthly_returns = 1 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 50 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_treasury = 30 }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.11.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.11.b executed"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = chi_bri_outcome
				value = 2
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_active_projects = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_completed_projects = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_global_presence = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 1 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 2 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 3 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 5 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 6 }
					check_variable = { FROM.project_type = 8 }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_monthly_returns = 1 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 20 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_treasury = 10 }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.11.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.11.c executed"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = chi_bri_outcome
				value = 3
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_active_projects = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_defaulted_projects = 1 }
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = bri_default_THIS
			country_event = { id = chi_bri.12 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

# chi_bri.12 -- Default Event (recipient scope, FROM = CHI)
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.12
	title = chi_bri.12.t
	desc = chi_bri.12.d

# chi_bri.20 -- Hambantota Handover (SRL scope, FROM = CHI)
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.20
	title = chi_bri.20.t
	desc = chi_bri.20.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_naval
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = SRL
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.20.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.20.a executed"
		413 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_bri_state_infrastructure }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_bri_state_infrastructure }
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_bri_state_infrastructure_controlled }
			set_state_flag = bri_port_413
		}
		set_country_flag = bri_default_THIS
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = medium_commercial_relations
		}
		FROM = {
			add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_predatory_score = 2 }
			set_country_flag = CHI_bri_hambantota_leased
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_stability < 0.35
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.20.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.20.b executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = negative_large_commercial_relations
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = negative_large_commercial_relations
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_stability > 0.6
			}
		}
	}
}

# chi_bri.41 -- Bilateral Signings (CHI scope)
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.41
	title = chi_bri.41.t
	desc = chi_bri.41.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_sign_treaty1
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = CHI
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.41.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.41.a executed"
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { original_tag = CHI }
				NOT = { original_tag = IND }
				NOT = { has_war_with = CHI }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = CHI_bri_pending_application }
				is_in_array = { array = global.bri_eligible_countries value = THIS }
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { array = global.bri_eligible_countries value = THIS }
					NOT = { original_tag = IND }
					NOT = { has_war_with = CHI }
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_bri_pending_application
				CHI = { country_event = { id = chi_bri.10 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_global_presence = 3 }
		country_event = { id = chi_bri.42 days = 2 }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		original_tag = CHI
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.70.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.70.a executed"

		if = {

				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bri_partner_tier_1 }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bri_partner_tier_2 }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = CHI
					modifier = large_commercial_relations
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = CHI_Bide_Your_Time }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = bri_partner_CHI
					capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = CHI
					modifier = large_commercial_relations
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_opinion_modifier = focac_member }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = diplomatic_charm
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = bri_partner_CHI
					capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bri_partner_tier_1 }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bri_partner_tier_2 }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = CHI
					modifier = large_commercial_relations
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = chi_bri.71 days = 7 }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

# chi_bri.95 -- CAI Aggression Check: Hidden Monthly Cancellation (CHI scope)
# Fired by D.4 focus completion (and re-fires itself every 30 days while CHI_eu_market_access is held).
# Cancels the CAI idea and swaps signatory modifiers to suspended on the 6 EU majors when
# CHI_chinese_aggression crosses 25. If the threshold is not met, schedules itself again.
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.95
	title = chi_bri.95.t
	desc = chi_bri.95.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.95.a
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CHI_eu_market_access
			check_variable = {
				var = CHI_chinese_aggression
				value = 25
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = CHI_eu_market_access
		GER = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_signatory }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_suspended }
		}
		FRA = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_signatory }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_suspended }
		}
		HOL = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_signatory }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_suspended }
		}
		BEL = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_signatory }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_suspended }
		}
		ITA = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_signatory }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_suspended }
		}
		SPR = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_signatory }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = CHI_cai_suspended }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.95.b
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CHI_eu_market_access
			check_variable = {
				var = CHI_chinese_aggression
				value = 25
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = chi_bri.95 days = 30 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

			modifier = { add = 5 has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 30 } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 has_war_with = FROM }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.133.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.133.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
	}
}

# chi_bri.134 -- CHI defender choice when a pacted party is at war with another pacted party (FROM = aggressor's victim, ROOT = CHI)
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.134
	title = chi_bri.134.t
	desc = chi_bri.134.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { original_tag = CHI }

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.134.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.134.a executed"
		add_political_power = -100
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = chi_bri.135 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 4
			modifier = { factor = 0 surrender_progress > 0.30 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.134.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.134.b executed"
		add_to_variable = { CHI_bri_winwin_score = -5 tooltip = CHI_bri_winwin_score_tt }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = chinese_betrayal }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
	}
}

# chi_bri.135 -- Notification to the victim of pacted war that CHI will honor the pact
country_event = {
	id = chi_bri.135
	title = chi_bri.135.t
	desc = chi_bri.135.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = chi_bri.135.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: chi_bri.135.a executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = chinese_pact_honored }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

# CHI Incident Events

country_event = {
	id = CHI_political_events.1
	title = CHI_political_events.1.t
	desc = CHI_political_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_crisis

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_political_events.1.a"
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = CHI_national_overall_emergency_response_plan }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = CHI_sars_response_effective_idea years = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = { idea = CHI_sars_outbreak_uncontrolled_idea years = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_political_system }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_pol_stability_factor = -0.05 tooltip = stability_factor_tt }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CHI_political_events.2
	title = CHI_political_events.2.t
	desc = CHI_political_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_crisis

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_political_events.2.a"
		586 = { add_manpower = -5000 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = CHI_national_overall_emergency_response_plan }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = CHI_wenchuan_reconstruction_drive_idea years = 2 }
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_political_system }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_pol_stability_factor = -0.05 tooltip = stability_factor_tt }
			add_to_variable = { CHI_pol_pp_gain = -0.05 tooltip = political_power_gain_tt }
		}
	}
}

	id = CHI_political_events.3

# CHI_two_centeraries — player chooses centenary focus direction
country_event = {
	id = CHI_political_events.4
	title = CHI_political_events.4.t
	desc = CHI_political_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_PLACEHOLDER

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.4.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_political_events.4.a"
		custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_political_system }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_pol_research_speed_factor = 0.03 tooltip = research_speed_factor_tt }
		newline = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_economy_modifier }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_economy_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = 0.05 tooltip = production_factory_max_efficiency_factor_tt }
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.4.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_political_events.4.b"
		custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_political_system }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_pol_consumer_goods_expected_value = -0.05 tooltip = consumer_goods_expected_value_tt }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_pol_expected_healthcare_modifier = 0.05 tooltip = expected_healthcare_modifier_tt }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_pol_expected_education_modifier = 0.05 tooltip = expected_education_modifier_tt }
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.4.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_political_events.4.c"
		add_country_leader_trait = CHI_two_centenary_supreme_commander
		newline = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = CHI_political_system }
		add_to_variable = { CHI_pol_war_support_factor = 0.05 tooltip = war_support_factor_tt }
	}
}

# CHI_designated_succesor — player chooses succession candidate based on factional balance
country_event = {
	id = CHI_political_events.5
	title = CHI_political_events.5.t
	desc = CHI_political_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_PLACEHOLDER

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.5.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_political_events.5.a"
		add_power_balance_value = { id = CHI_factional_balance value = 0.10 tooltip_side = CHI_tuanpai_youth_league }
		add_political_power = 25
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.5.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_political_events.5.b"
		add_power_balance_value = { id = CHI_factional_balance value = -0.10 tooltip_side = CHI_princeling_shanghai }
		add_political_power = 25
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI_political_events.5.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: CHI_political_events.5.c"
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}
